to refugees, however he also shares disagreement with proposed quotas.<sup id="cite_ref-247" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-247"><span>[</span>245<span>]</span></a></sup> Former <a href="/wiki/Minister_of_Foreign_Affairs_of_the_Czech_Republic" title="Minister of Foreign Affairs of the Czech Republic" class="mw-redirect">Minister of Foreign Affairs</a> <a href="/wiki/Karel_Schwarzenberg" title="Karel Schwarzenberg">Karel Schwarzenberg</a> has said the country should take in 80,000 refugees.<sup id="cite_ref-248" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-248"><span>[</span>246<span>]</span></a></sup> Minister of Human Rights and Equal Opportunities <a href="/wiki/Ji%C5%99%C3%AD_Dienstbier_Jr." title="Jiří Dienstbier Jr.">Jiří Dienstbier</a> said the country is able to accept 7,000 —15,000 refugees now and should express solidarity and help other countries facing the strongest influx of refugees without quotas.<sup id="cite_ref-249" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-249"><span>[</span>247<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Flag_of_Denmark.svg/20px-Flag_of_Denmark.svg.png" width="20" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Flag_of_Denmark.svg/31px-Flag_of_Denmark.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Flag_of_Denmark.svg/40px-Flag_of_Denmark.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="370" data-file-height="280" />&#160;</span>Denmark – Denmark closed the <a href="/wiki/European_route_E45" title="European route E45">E45 Motorway</a> and rail links with Germany to stop migrants from illegally entering the country.<sup id="cite_ref-250" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-250"><span>[</span>248<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Flag_of_Finland.svg/23px-Flag_of_Finland.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Flag_of_Finland.svg/35px-Flag_of_Finland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bc/Flag_of_Finland.svg/46px-Flag_of_Finland.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1800" data-file-height="1100" />&#160;</span>Finland – On 14 September, a former prime minister <a href="/wiki/Matti_Vanhanen" title="Matti Vanhanen">Matti Vanhanen</a> noted that the government needed to regain control on who enters the country and to divert asylum seekers to special camps. He did not think that it would be appropriate that the asylum seekers could continue to freely move around.<sup id="cite_ref-251" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-251"><span>[</span>249<span>]</span></a></sup> Later on the same day, the Minister of the Interior <a href="/wiki/Petteri_Orpo" title="Petteri Orpo">Petteri Orpo</a>, who is also a member of the National Coalition Party, noted that tightened border controls would be imposed on the northern border stations by the end of the week.<sup id="cite_ref-252" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-252"><span>[</span>250<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/23px-Flag_of_France.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/35px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/c/c3/Flag_of_France.svg/45px-Flag_of_France.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>France – On 23 September, after the Czech Republic, Hungary, Romania, and Slovakia voted against a plan to relocate asylum-seekers arriving in Greece, Italy, and Hungary among other member states, French President <a href="/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Hollande" title="François Hollande">François Hollande</a> warned former <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Bloc" title="Eastern Bloc">Eastern Bloc</a> countries against rejecting the EU mandatory migrant quotas: "Those who don't share our values, those who don't even want to respect those principles, need to start asking themselves questions about their place in the European Union."<sup id="cite_ref-253" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-253"><span>[</span>251<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/23px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/35px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/ba/Flag_of_Germany.svg/46px-Flag_of_Germany.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>Germany – Vice Chancellor <a href="/wiki/Sigmar_Gabriel" title="Sigmar Gabriel">Sigmar Gabriel</a> said that Germany could take in 500,000 refugees annually for the next several years.<sup id="cite_ref-254" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-254"><span>[</span>252<span>]</span></a></sup> German opposition to the government's admission of the new wave of migrants has been an increasingly tense political debate, coupled with a rise in anti-immigration protests.<sup id="cite_ref-Hill_255-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hill-255"><span>[</span>253<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Pegida" title="Pegida">Pegida</a>, an anti-immigration movement flourished briefly in late 2014, followed by a new wave of anti-immigration protests in the late summer of 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-Fenton_256-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fenton-256"><span>[</span>254<span>]</span></a></sup> Chancellor <a href="/wiki/Angela_Merkel" title="Angela Merkel">Angela Merkel</a> insisted that Germany has the economic strength to cope with the influx of migrants and reiterated that there is no legal maximum limit on the number of migrants Germany can take.<sup id="cite_ref-257" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-257"><span>[</span>255<span>]</span></a></sup> In September 2015, enthusiastic crowds across the country welcomed arriving refugees and migrants. <a href="/wiki/Christian_Social_Union_in_Bavaria" title="Christian Social Union in Bavaria">Christian Social Union in Bavaria</a>, the sister party of Merkel's <a href="/wiki/Christian_Democratic_Union_of_Germany" title="Christian Democratic Union of Germany">Christian Democratic Union</a> called Merkel's decisions "wrong",<sup id="cite_ref-258" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-258"><span>[</span>256<span>]</span></a></sup> while <a href="/wiki/Yasmin_Fahimi" title="Yasmin Fahimi">Yasmin Fahimi</a>, secretary-general of the <a href="/wiki/Social_Democratic_Party_of_Germany" title="Social Democratic Party of Germany">Social Democratic Party</a>, the junior partner of the ruling coalition, praised Merkel's policy allowing migrants in Hungary to enter Germany as "a strong signal of humanity to show that Europe's values are valid also in difficult times".<sup id="cite_ref-259" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-259"><span>[</span>257<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/North_Rhine-Westphalia" title="North Rhine-Westphalia">North Rhine-Westphalia</a>, Germany's most populous state, was hiring more than 3,600 new teachers to manage the influx of an estimated 40,000 new refugee children in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-260" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-260"><span>[</span>258<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Christian_Social_Union_in_Bavaria" title="Christian Social Union in Bavaria">CSU</a> leader and <a href="/wiki/Bavaria" title="Bavaria">Bavarian</a> State Premier <a href="/wiki/Horst_Seehofer" title="Horst Seehofer">Horst Seehofer</a> criticized Merkel's decision to allow in migrants: "We’re now in a state of mind without rules, without system and without order because of a German decision."<sup id="cite_ref-261" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-261"><span>[</span>259<span>]</span></a></sup> The German Interior Ministry estimates as many as 30% of asylum seekers arriving in Germany claiming to be from Syria are in fact from other countries.<sup id="cite_ref-262" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-262"><span>[</span>260<span>]</span></a></sup> Merkel's government wants to impose <a href="/wiki/Economic_sanctions" title="Economic sanctions">economic sanctions</a> on European Union countries that reject mandatory refugee quotas.<sup id="cite_ref-263" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-263"><span>[</span>261<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>

Migrants crossing illegaly into Hungary underneath the unfinished <a href="/wiki/Hungary%E2%80%93Serbia_border_fence" title="Hungary–Serbia border fence" class="mw-redirect">Hungary–Serbia border fence</a>, 25 August 2015</div>

<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Flag_of_Hungary.svg/23px-Flag_of_Hungary.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Flag_of_Hungary.svg/35px-Flag_of_Hungary.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c1/Flag_of_Hungary.svg/46px-Flag_of_Hungary.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>Hungary – Hungary has finished construction of the first phase of a <a href="/wiki/Hungary%E2%80%93Serbia_border_fence" title="Hungary–Serbia border fence" class="mw-redirect">fence</a> on its southern border with Serbia in late August 2015, according to the Hungarian Ministry of Defence. The fence consists of three strands of NATO razor wire, and is 175 kilometers long. The next phase involves construction of a wire fence which will be approximately 4 meters high. In August, describing Hungary as, "under siege from human traffickers", Minister of the Prime Minister's Office <a href="/wiki/J%C3%A1nos_L%C3%A1z%C3%A1r" title="János Lázár">János Lázár</a> announces that the government would "defend this stretch of our borders with force", deploying 9,000 police to keep undocumented migrants out.<sup id="cite_ref-BorderHunters_264-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BorderHunters-264"><span>[</span>262<span>]</span></a></sup> Hungary's Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Orb%C3%A1n" title="Viktor Orbán">Viktor Orbán</a> wrote in the <i><a href="/wiki/Frankfurter_Allgemeine_Zeitung" title="Frankfurter Allgemeine Zeitung">Frankfurter Allgemeine Zeitung</a></i>: "Europe’s response is madness. We must acknowledge that the European Union's misguided immigration policy is responsible for this situation."<sup id="cite_ref-265" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-265"><span>[</span>263<span>]</span></a></sup> Orbán also demanded an official EU list of "safe countries" to which migrants can be returned.<sup id="cite_ref-266" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-266"><span>[</span>264<span>]</span></a></sup> He said that "the moral, human thing is to make clear: ‘Please don’t come. Why do you have to go from Turkey to Europe? Turkey is a safe country. Stay there. It’s risky to come.’"<sup id="cite_ref-267" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-267"><span>[</span>265<span>]</span></a></sup> Speaking at <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">United Nations General Assembly</a>, Orbán called for "global quota" system to distribute refugees to all countries.<sup id="cite_ref-268" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-268"><span>[</span>266<span>]</span></a></sup>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:P31_L.%C3%89._Eithne_Operations_28_June_2015.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/P31_L.%C3%89._Eithne_Operations_28_June_2015.jpg/220px-P31_L.%C3%89._Eithne_Operations_28_June_2015.jpg" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/P31_L.%C3%89._Eithne_Operations_28_June_2015.jpg/330px-P31_L.%C3%89._Eithne_Operations_28_June_2015.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/P31_L.%C3%89._Eithne_Operations_28_June_2015.jpg/440px-P31_L.%C3%89._Eithne_Operations_28_June_2015.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4928" data-file-height="3280" /></a>

Rescued migrants are brought to southern Italian ports, 28 June 2015</div>

</div>
</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/03/Flag_of_Italy.svg/23px-Flag_of_Italy.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/03/Flag_of_Italy.svg/35px-Flag_of_Italy.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/03/Flag_of_Italy.svg/45px-Flag_of_Italy.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1500" data-file-height="1000" />&#160;</span>Italy – Some Italian towns and cities have refused instructions from the national government to house migrants.<sup id="cite_ref-Legorno_269-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Legorno-269"><span>[</span>267<span>]</span></a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Mafia_Capitale_investigation" title="Mafia Capitale investigation">Mafia Capitale investigation</a> revealed that the <a href="/wiki/Organized_crime_in_Italy" title="Organized crime in Italy">Italian Mafia</a> profits from the migrant crisis and exploits refugees.<sup id="cite_ref-270" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-270"><span>[</span>268<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-271" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-271"><span>[</span>269<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Pope_Francis" title="Pope Francis">Pope Francis</a> thanked the <a href="/wiki/Italian_navy" title="Italian navy" class="mw-redirect">Italian navy</a> for migrant rescue effort.<sup id="cite_ref-272" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-272"><span>[</span>270<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Flag_of_Latvia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Latvia.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Flag_of_Latvia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Latvia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Flag_of_Latvia.svg/46px-Flag_of_Latvia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>Latvia – Latvia decided to receive 250 migrants in the next two years according to the EU plan. <a href="/wiki/National_Alliance_(Latvia)" title="National Alliance (Latvia)">National Alliance party</a> expressed its disapproval of such decision. On 4 August 2015 around 250 activists gathered in <a href="/wiki/Riga" title="Riga">Riga</a> on a protest against Government's decision on receiving migrants.</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Flag_of_Lithuania.svg/23px-Flag_of_Lithuania.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Flag_of_Lithuania.svg/35px-Flag_of_Lithuania.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Flag_of_Lithuania.svg/46px-Flag_of_Lithuania.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="300" />&#160;</span>Lithuania – Lithuania decided to receive 325 migrants, although after the increase of migrant flow in August 2015, its government did not discount the possibility of accepting a greater number of migrants later in the same year.<sup id="cite_ref-DELFI_273-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DELFI-273"><span>[</span>271<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Malta.svg/23px-Flag_of_Malta.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Malta.svg/35px-Flag_of_Malta.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Malta.svg/45px-Flag_of_Malta.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>Malta – Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Muscat" title="Joseph Muscat">Joseph Muscat</a> called the crisis "an ugly period" for Europe, and said that Malta will take in 75 migrants from Italy and Greece.<sup id="cite_ref-274" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-274"><span>[</span>272<span>]</span></a></sup> He also called for a 'global system of refugee quotas'.<sup id="cite_ref-275" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-275"><span>[</span>273<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/1/12/Flag_of_Poland.svg/23px-Flag_of_Poland.svg.png" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/1/12/Flag_of_Poland.svg/35px-Flag_of_Poland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/1/12/Flag_of_Poland.svg/46px-Flag_of_Poland.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="800" />&#160;</span>Poland – Government officials stated that the country is ready to take 2,000 refugees.<sup id="cite_ref-276" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-276"><span>[</span>274<span>]</span></a></sup> Polish President <a href="/wiki/Andrzej_Duda" title="Andrzej Duda">Andrzej Duda</a> rejected the European Union's proposal of compulsory migrant quotas, saying: "I won’t agree to a dictate of the strong. I won’t back a Europe where the economic advantage of the size of a population will be a reason to force solutions on other countries regardless of their national interests".<sup id="cite_ref-277" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-277"><span>[</span>275<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Portugal.svg/23px-Flag_of_Portugal.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Portugal.svg/35px-Flag_of_Portugal.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Flag_of_Portugal.svg/45px-Flag_of_Portugal.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="400" />&#160;</span>Portugal – In the next two years, Portugal is willing to offer shelter to 1,500 of the refugees flooding into Europe from the Mediterranean Sea. A source has told Diário de Notícias that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has already presented its counter-proposal to the European Commission (EC), which wanted Portugal to absorb 2,400 refugees.<sup id="cite_ref-278" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-278"><span>[</span>276<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Romania.svg/23px-Flag_of_Romania.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Romania.svg/35px-Flag_of_Romania.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Flag_of_Romania.svg/45px-Flag_of_Romania.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="400" />&#160;</span>Romania – The <a href="/wiki/European_Commission" title="European Commission">European Commission</a> asked Romania to accept 6,351 refugees under an EU quota scheme. The EurActiv reported that "Romanian Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Victor_Ponta" title="Victor Ponta">Victor Ponta</a> said that his country will request admission to the EU's <a href="/wiki/Schengen_Area" title="Schengen Area">Schengen borderless area</a> if mandatory quotas to accept refugees are decided by the Union".<sup id="cite_ref-279" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-279"><span>[</span>277<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Flag_of_Slovakia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Slovakia.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Flag_of_Slovakia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Slovakia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Flag_of_Slovakia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Slovakia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>Slovakia – Government of Slovakia stated that it would help with migration into Europe by receiving 200 migrants according to the EU plan, but on condition that the migrants are <a href="/wiki/Christianity" title="Christianity">Christians</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Troianoski_280-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Troianoski-280"><span>[</span>278<span>]</span></a></sup> Slovak Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Robert_Fico" title="Robert Fico">Robert Fico</a> said: "I have only one question: who bombed Libya? Who caused problems in North Africa? Slovakia? No!" The Prime Minister proposed temporary refuge in his country for 500 migrants who have submitted requests for asylum in Austria, whose accommodation for refugees is overfilled, but as for 200 migrants that Slovakia will receive according to the EU plan, requires that these 500 are Christians as well. On 15 September 2015, Fico was reported saying that all crossing the border illegally would be detained.<sup id="cite_ref-281" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-281"><span>[</span>279<span>]</span></a></sup> Fico rejected European Commission plan to distribute migrants among EU member states, saying: "As long as I am prime minister, mandatory quotas will not be implemented on Slovak territory."<sup id="cite_ref-282" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-282"><span>[</span>280<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Progressive_Alliance_of_Socialists_and_Democrats" title="Progressive Alliance of Socialists and Democrats">S&amp;D</a> Group leader has proposed to suspend Fico's <a href="/wiki/Direction_%E2%80%93_Social_Democracy" title="Direction – Social Democracy">SMER</a> party from the <a href="/wiki/Party_of_European_Socialists" title="Party of European Socialists">Party of European Socialists</a> (PES).<sup id="cite_ref-283" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-283"><span>[</span>281<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>United Kingdom – British Home Secretary <a href="/wiki/Theresa_May" title="Theresa May">Theresa May</a> said that it was important to help people living in war zones regions and refugee camps but "not the ones who are strong and rich enough to come to Europe".<sup id="cite_ref-284" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-284"><span>[</span>282<span>]</span></a></sup> British opposition politician <a href="/wiki/Nigel_Farage" title="Nigel Farage">Nigel Farage</a> stated that the exodus from Libya had been caused by <a href="/wiki/2011_military_intervention_in_Libya" title="2011 military intervention in Libya">NATO military intervention</a>, approved by <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> and Nicolas Sarkozy, in the <a href="/wiki/Libyan_Crisis_(2011%E2%80%93present)" title="Libyan Crisis (2011–present)">civil war in Libya</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-285" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-285"><span>[</span>283<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="International">International</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_migrant_crisis&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: International">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>The United Nations predicted that one million migrants should reach Europe by 2016<sup id="cite_ref-286" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-286"><span>[</span>284<span>]</span></a></sup> and warned on 25 September 2015 that worsening conditions in Iraq would send new waves of migrants to Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-287" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-287"><span>[</span>285<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> Secretary General <a href="/wiki/Jens_Stoltenberg" title="Jens Stoltenberg">Jens Stoltenberg</a> said that "there is a need for immediate measures, border, migrant, the discussion about quotas, so on – this is civilian issues, addressed by the European Union."<sup id="cite_ref-288" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-288"><span>[</span>286<span>]</span></a></sup> Czech Deputy Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Andrej_Babi%C5%A1" title="Andrej Babiš">Andrej Babiš</a> said in reaction: "According to the NATO chief, the problem of refugees is a problem of the EU and the border protection and the fight against people smugglers is in the power of particular EU member states."<sup id="cite_ref-CN_246-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CN-246"><span>[</span>244<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>The Russian Federation released an official statement on 2 September 2015 that the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> was working on a draft resolution to address the European migrant crisis, likely by permitting the inspection of suspected migrant ships.<sup id="cite_ref-UNSecurityCouncilMigrantCrisis_289-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UNSecurityCouncilMigrantCrisis-289"><span>[</span>287<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>The International Organization for Migration says that deaths at sea have increased ninefold after the end of <a href="/wiki/Operation_Mare_Nostrum" title="Operation Mare Nostrum">Operation Mare Nostrum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-290" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-290"><span>[</span>288<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Amnesty_International" title="Amnesty International">Amnesty International</a> condemned European governments for "negligence towards the humanitarian crisis in the Mediterranean" which they say has led to an increase in deaths at sea.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amnesty_International" title="Amnesty International">Amnesty International</a> and <a href="/wiki/Human_Rights_Watch" title="Human Rights Watch">Human Rights Watch</a> have criticised the funding of search and rescue operations. Amnesty International says that the EU is "turning its back on its responsibilities and clearly threatening thousands of lives".<sup id="cite_ref-291" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-291"><span>[</span>289<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-292" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-292"><span>[</span>290<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>In 4 September 2015, <a href="/wiki/Euro-_Mediterranean_Human_Rights_Monitor" title="Euro- Mediterranean Human Rights Monitor">Euro- Mediterranean Human Rights Monitor</a> published a new report entitled “THE EU REFUGEE CRISIS IN NUMBERS<sup id="cite_ref-293" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-293"><span>[</span>291<span>]</span></a></sup>”. The report provides a numerical data on the number of refugees who fled their homelands, seeking for a better life. The report confirms that <a href="/wiki/July" title="July">July</a> and August witnessed the peak of the number of <a href="/wiki/Migrant" title="Migrant" class="mw-disambig">migrants</a>. During the first eight months,380,000 refugees arrived Europe while 190,000 migrants arrived <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">Europe</a> in July and August alone. Sandra Owen, the observer of irregular migration for Euro-Med Monitor, calls the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">EU</a> for an urgent intervention to end this misery. The Euro-Med also attracts the attention of the European governments that closing the borders and building walls are useless directives, calling for providing safe asylums for those migrants.</li>
</ul>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Syrian_refugees_in_the_Middle_East_map_en.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Syrian_refugees_in_the_Middle_East_map_en.svg/300px-Syrian_refugees_in_the_Middle_East_map_en.svg.png" width="300" height="197" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Syrian_refugees_in_the_Middle_East_map_en.svg/450px-Syrian_refugees_in_the_Middle_East_map_en.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Syrian_refugees_in_the_Middle_East_map_en.svg/600px-Syrian_refugees_in_the_Middle_East_map_en.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="839" data-file-height="552" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Syrian_refugees_in_the_Middle_East_map_en.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War_refugees" title="Syrian Civil War refugees" class="mw-redirect">Syrian Civil War refugees</a> in neighboring countries (as of 4 September 2015)<sup id="cite_ref-294" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-294"><span>[</span>292<span>]</span></a></sup></div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li>In August 2015, <a href="/wiki/Amnesty_International" title="Amnesty International">Amnesty International</a> reported that <a href="/wiki/Qatar" title="Qatar">Qatar</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">United Arab Emirates</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kuwait" title="Kuwait">Kuwait</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahrain</a> have offered "zero resettlement places to Syrian refugees", although they gave some money to refugee aid initiatives.<sup id="cite_ref-295" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-295"><span>[</span>293<span>]</span></a></sup> According to some analysis, Saudi Arabia and its <a href="/wiki/Gulf_Cooperation_Council" title="Gulf Cooperation Council">Gulf Cooperation Council</a> allies could easily take up to three million Syrian refugees within one year.<sup id="cite_ref-296" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-296"><span>[</span>294<span>]</span></a></sup> The BBC reported that "most successful cases are Syrians already in Gulf states extending their stays, or those entering because they have family there."<sup id="cite_ref-bbc.com_297-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbc.com-297"><span>[</span>295<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a> offered to <a href="/wiki/Petro-Islam" title="Petro-Islam">build 200 new mosques</a> for Muslim refugees in Germany.<sup id="cite_ref-298" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-298"><span>[</span>296<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>Australian PM <a href="/wiki/Tony_Abbott" title="Tony Abbott">Tony Abbott</a> said the tragedies were "worsened by Europe's refusal to learn from its own mistakes and from the efforts of others who have handled similar problems. Destroying the criminal people-smugglers was the centre of gravity of our border control policies, and judicious boat turnbacks was the key."<sup id="cite_ref-299" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-299"><span>[</span>297<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pope_Francis" title="Pope Francis">Pope Francis</a> expressed his concern about the loss of life and urged EU leaders to "act decisively and quickly to stop these tragedies from recurring".<sup id="cite_ref-abc_300-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-abc-300"><span>[</span>298<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On 4 September 2015, the Israeli Opposition leader <a href="/wiki/Isaac_Herzog" title="Isaac Herzog">Isaac Herzog</a> called on Israel to accept refugees from Syria, in addition to the humanitarian efforts it is already making.<sup id="cite_ref-301" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-301"><span>[</span>299<span>]</span></a></sup> Two days later, Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu" title="Benjamin Netanyahu">Benjamin Netanyahu</a> rejected calls to accept Syrian refugees, attributing a lack of "demographic and geographic depth" for Israel to accommodate them.<sup id="cite_ref-302" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-302"><span>[</span>300<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On 7 September 2015, it was reported that <a href="/wiki/Pope_Benedict_XVI" title="Pope Benedict XVI">Pope Benedict XVI</a> was "praying for migrants and refugees" from <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>. He said that “Unfortunately the sea for many has become a tomb, but it should be a bridge. It must not be considered a border: the sea connects one country to another, one continent to another. If there are problems in a country or in a continent, the opposite shore should be there to help”.<sup id="cite_ref-303" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-303"><span>[</span>301<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a>'s Education Minister <a href="/wiki/Elias_Bou_Saab" title="Elias Bou Saab">Elias Bou Saab</a> told British Prime Minister David Cameron that "as many as 2% of the refugees could be jihadis belonging to Islamic State [Isis]".<sup id="cite_ref-304" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-304"><span>[</span>302<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> praised Germany for taking a leading role in accepting refugees.<sup id="cite_ref-305" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-305"><span>[</span>303<span>]</span></a></sup> In September 2015, he decided to raise the number of Syrian refugees admitted in the USA to at least 10,000 in 2016 from less than 2,000 in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-306" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-306"><span>[</span>304<span>]</span></a></sup> Syrians would be part of an increase in the total number of worldwide refugees taken in by the USA each year – major refugee groups resettling in the United States are from Iraq, Burma, Somalia, <a href="/wiki/Bhutanese_refugees" title="Bhutanese refugees">Bhutan</a> and the Democratic Republic of the Congo<sup id="cite_ref-307" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-307"><span>[</span>305<span>]</span></a></sup> – from 70,000 in 2015 to 85,000 in 2016 and 100,000 in 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-308" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-308"><span>[</span>306<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>American billionaire and presidential candidate <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> said that the United States should take in Syrian refugees, putting the blame for their plight on <a href="/wiki/Foreign_policy_of_the_Barack_Obama_administration" title="Foreign policy of the Barack Obama administration">Obama's foreign policy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-309" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-309"><span>[</span>307<span>]</span></a></sup> Later, Trump has said that if elected he would deport all Syrian refugees because they may be ISIS supporters in disguise.<sup id="cite_ref-310" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-310"><span>[</span>308<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> refused to admit refugees affected by conflicts in the Middle East and Africa. Japanese Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Shinz%C5%8D_Abe" title="Shinzō Abe">Shinzō Abe</a> stated, "We must raise our birth rate. There are many things that we should do before accepting immigrants."<sup id="cite_ref-311" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-311"><span>[</span>309<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Health_guidance">Health guidance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_migrant_crisis&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Health guidance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote relarticle mainarticle">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Migrant_health" title="Migrant health">Migrant health</a></div>
<p>Prevention care for people affected by conflict, poverty, and migration should be informed by country of origin and migration history.<sup id="cite_ref-Pottie2011_312-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pottie2011-312"><span>[</span>310<span>]</span></a></sup> Forced migration, low income, and limited ability in the host country language increases risk for decline in health.<sup id="cite_ref-Pottie2011_312-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pottie2011-312"><span>[</span>310<span>]</span></a></sup> While access to sufficient housing, employment, income, keeping parents and children together have protective health effects. Vaccination with <a href="/wiki/MMR_vaccine" title="MMR vaccine">MMR vaccine</a>, <a href="/wiki/DPT_vaccine" title="DPT vaccine">DPT vaccine</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Polio_vaccine" title="Polio vaccine">polio vaccine</a> is recommended for all children and adults.<sup id="cite_ref-Pottie2011_312-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pottie2011-312"><span>[</span>310<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Varicella_vaccination" title="Varicella vaccination" class="mw-redirect">Varicella vaccination</a> is recommended for those from tropical areas.<sup id="cite_ref-Pottie2011_312-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pottie2011-312"><span>[</span>310<span>]</span></a></sup> Migrant populations face barriers and benefit from help in accessing health and social services.<sup id="cite_ref-Pottie2011_312-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pottie2011-312"><span>[</span>310<span>]</span></a></sup> Primary care nurses and physicians report <a href="/wiki/Evidence_based_guidelines" title="Evidence based guidelines" class="mw-redirect">evidence based guidelines</a> helped in the delivery of care for new refugees.<sup id="cite_ref-Delphi_313-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Delphi-313"><span>[</span>311<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>Trauma-exposed individuals often receive treatment called <a href="/w/index.php?title=Psychological_debriefing&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Psychological debriefing (page does not exist)">psychological debriefing</a> in an effort to prevent <a href="/wiki/Post_traumatic_stress_disorder" title="Post traumatic stress disorder" class="mw-redirect">post traumatic stress disorder</a> (PTSD).<sup id="cite_ref-Feldner2007_314-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Feldner2007-314"><span>[</span>312<span>]</span></a></sup> Several <a href="/wiki/Meta-analysis" title="Meta-analysis">meta-analyses</a>; however, find that psychological debriefing is unhelpful and is potentially harmful.<sup id="cite_ref-Feldner2007_314-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Feldner2007-314"><span>[</span>312<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-315" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-315"><span>[</span>313<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-316" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-316"><span>[</span>314<span>]</span></a></sup> This is true for both single-session debriefing and multiple session interventions.<sup id="cite_ref-317" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-317"><span>[</span>315<span>]</span></a></sup> Additional general screening for traumatic events is not recommended.<sup id="cite_ref-Pottie2011_312-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pottie2011-312"><span>[</span>310<span>]</span></a></sup> Interactions with people affect by trauma should involve being <a href="/wiki/Empathetic" title="Empathetic" class="mw-redirect">empathetic</a>, providing reassurance, and providing support.<sup id="cite_ref-Pottie2011_312-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pottie2011-312"><span>[</span>310<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Political_debate">Political debate</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_migrant_crisis&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Political debate">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="European_People.27s_Party">European People's Party</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_migrant_crisis&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: European People's Party">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quotebox" style="float: right; clear: right; margin: 0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em; width:30%; padding: 6px; border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 88%; background-color: #F9F9F9;">
<div class="" style="position: relative; text-align: left;">
<div style="margin:0px 2em;">
<p>Europe needs to fulfil its humanitarian duty, helping those fleeing for their lives, and as a Christian-Democrat, I want to reiterate that is not Christian rights, but human rights that Europe invented. But we also need to better secure our external borders and make sure that asylum rules are used properly and not abused.</p>
</div>
<div style="position: absolute; left: 0px; top: 0px; text-align: left; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; font-size: large; color: gray;">“</div>
<div style="position: absolute; right: 0px; bottom: 0px; text-align: left; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; font-size: large; color: gray;">”</div>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;"><cite>— <a href="/wiki/Manfred_Weber" title="Manfred Weber">Manfred Weber</a>, leader of the <a href="/wiki/European_People%27s_Party" title="European People's Party">European People's Party</a> in the European Parliament.</cite></div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/European_Commission" title="European Commission">European Commissioner</a> for Migration, Home Affairs and Citizenship, <a href="/wiki/Dimitris_Avramopoulos" title="Dimitris Avramopoulos">Dimitris Avramopoulos</a>, said that the European Commission "does not care about the political cost" of its handling of the migration crisis, because it's there for five years to do its job "with vision, responsibility and commitment" and what drives it "is not to be re-elected", and invited European national leaders to do likewise and stop worrying about reelection.<sup id="cite_ref-318" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-318"><span>[</span>316<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-319" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-319"><span>[</span>317<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Christian_Democratic_Union_of_Germany" title="Christian Democratic Union of Germany">Christian Democratic Union of Germany</a> – On 31 August 2015, according to <i>The New York Times</i>, <a href="/wiki/Chancellor_of_Germany" title="Chancellor of Germany">Chancellor</a> <a href="/wiki/Angela_Merkel" title="Angela Merkel">Angela Merkel</a> of Germany, in some of her strongest language theretofore on the immigrant crisis, warned that freedom of travel and open borders among the 28 member states of the EU could be jeopardised if they did not agree on a shared response to this crisis.<sup id="cite_ref-StrainedOpenBorders_141-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-StrainedOpenBorders-141"><span>[</span>139<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/The_Republicans_(France)" title="The Republicans (France)">The Republicans (France)</a> – <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Sarkozy" title="Nicolas Sarkozy">Nicolas Sarkozy</a> compared EU migrant plan to "mending a burst pipe by spreading water round the house while leaving the leak untouched".<sup id="cite_ref-320" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-320"><span>[</span>318<span>]</span></a></sup> Following German Chancellor Angela Merkel's decision to allow tens of thousands of people to enter Germany, Sarkozy criticized her, saying that it would attract even greater amounts of people to Europe, where a significant part would "inevitably" end up in France due to the EU's free movement policies and the French welfare state. He also demanded that the Schengen agreement on borderless travel should be replaced with a new agreement providing border checks for non-EU citizens.<sup id="cite_ref-321" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-321"><span>[</span>319<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Party_of_European_Socialists">Party of European Socialists</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_migrant_crisis&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Party of European Socialists">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quotebox" style="float: right; clear: right; margin: 0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em; width:30%; padding: 6px; border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 88%; background-color: #F9F9F9;">
<div class="" style="position: relative; text-align: left;">
<div style="margin:0px 2em;">
<p>At this moment, more people in the world are displaced by conflict than at any time since the Second World War. ... Many die on the approach to Europe – in the Mediterranean – yet others perish on European soil. ... As social democrats the principle of solidarity is the glue that keeps our family together. ... We need a permanent European mechanism for fairly distributing asylum-seekers in European member states. ... War, poverty and the stark rise in inequality are global, not local problems. As long as we do not address these causes globally, we cannot deny people the right to look for a more hopeful future in a safer environment.</p>
</div>
<div style="position: absolute; left: 0px; top: 0px; text-align: left; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; font-size: large; color: gray;">“</div>
<div style="position: absolute; right: 0px; bottom: 0px; text-align: left; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; font-size: large; color: gray;">”</div>
</div>
<div style="text-align: left;"><cite>— <a href="/wiki/Sergei_Stanishev" title="Sergei Stanishev">Sergei Stanishev</a>, President of the <a href="/wiki/Party_of_European_Socialists" title="Party of European Socialists">Party of European Socialists</a><sup id="cite_ref-322" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-322"><span>[</span>320<span>]</span></a></sup></cite></div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(Italy)" title="Democratic Party (Italy)">Democratic Party (Italy)</a> – <a href="/wiki/Italian_Prime_Minister" title="Italian Prime Minister" class="mw-redirect">Italian Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Matteo_Renzi" title="Matteo Renzi">Matteo Renzi</a> said the EU should forge a single European policy on asylum.<sup id="cite_ref-323" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-323"><span>[</span>321<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Socialist_Party_(France)" title="Socialist Party (France)">Socialist Party (France)</a> – <a href="/wiki/French_Prime_Minister" title="French Prime Minister" class="mw-redirect">French Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Valls" title="Manuel Valls">Manuel Valls</a> stated, "There must be close cooperation between the European Commission and member states as well as candidate members."<sup id="cite_ref-324" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-324"><span>[</span>322<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Eurosceptic_parties">Eurosceptic parties</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=European_migrant_crisis&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Eurosceptic parties">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>According to <i><a href="/wiki/The_Wall_Street_Journal" title="The Wall Street Journal">The Wall Street Journal</a></i>, the appeal of <a href="/wiki/Eurosceptic" title="Eurosceptic" class="mw-redirect">Eurosceptic</a> politicians has increased.<sup id="cite_ref-Troianoski_280-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Troianoski-280"><span>[</span>278<span>]</span></a></sup> On 10 September 2015, <a href="/wiki/The_Times" title="The Times">The Times</a> (UK) reported that French anti-EU politician <a href="/wiki/Marine_Le_Pen" title="Marine Le Pen">Marine Le Pen</a> is "on course for presidency".<sup id="cite_ref-325" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-325"><span>[</span>323<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nigel_Farage" title="Nigel Farage">Nigel Farage</a>, leader of the British anti-EU <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom_Independence_Party" title="United Kingdom Independence Party" class="mw-redirect">United Kingdom Independence Party</a> and co-leader of the eurosceptic <a href="/wiki/Europe_of_Freedom_and_Direct_Democracy" title="Europe of Freedom and Direct Democracy">Europe of Freedom and Direct Democracy</a> group, blamed the EU "and Germany in particular" for giving "huge incentives for people to come to the European Union by whatever means" and said that this would make deaths more likely. Additionally, he said that the EU's Schengen agreement on open borders had failed and warned that Islamists could exploit the situation and enter Europe in large numbers, pointing out that "one of the Isil terrorist suspects who committed the first atrocity against holidaymakers in <a href="/wiki/Tunisia" title="Tunisia">Tunisia</a> has been seen getting off a boat onto Italian soil".<sup id="cite_ref-326" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-326"><span>[</span>324<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-327" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-327"><span>[</span>325<span>]</span></a></sup> In 2013, Farage had called on the UK government to accept more Syrian refugees,<sup id="cite_ref-328" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-328"><span>[</span>326<span>]</span></a></sup> before clarifying that those refugees should be Christian due to the existence of nearer places of refuge for Muslims.<sup id="cite_ref-329" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-329"><span>[</span>327<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Europe_of_Nations_and_Freedom" title="Europe of Nations and Freedom">Europe of Nations and Freedom</a> Co-President <a href="/wiki/Marine_Le_Pen" title="Marine Le Pen">Marine Le Pen</a>, leader of the French far-right <a href="/wiki/National_Front_(France)" title="National Front (France)">National Front</a>, accused Germany of looking to hire "slaves" by opening its doors to large numbers of asylum seekers among a debate in Germany whether there should be exceptions to the recently introduced minimum wage law for refugees.<sup id="cite_ref-330" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-330"><span>[</span>328<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-331" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-331"><span>[</span>329<span>]</span></a></sup> Le Pen also accused Germany of imposing its immigration policy on the rest of the EU unilaterally.<sup id="cite_ref-332" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-332"><span>[</span>330<span>]</span></a></sup> Her comments were reported by the German<sup id="cite_ref-333" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-333"><span>[</span>331<span>]</span></a></sup> and Austrian press,<sup id="cite_ref-334" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-334"><span>[</span>332<span>]</span></a></sup> and were called "abstruse claims" by the online edition of <i><a href="/wiki/Der_Spiegel" title="Der Spiegel">Der Spiegel</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-335" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-335"><span>[</span>333<span>]</span></a></sup> Centre-right daily <i><a href="/wiki/Die_Welt" title="Die Welt">Die Welt</a></i> wrote that she "exploits the refugee crisis for anti-German propaganda".<sup id="cite_ref-336" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-336"><span>[</span>334<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Geert_Wilders" title="Geert Wilders">Geert Wilders</a>, the leader of the Dutch <a href="/wiki/Party_for_Freedom" title="Party for Freedom">Party for Freedom</a> (a member of Europe of Nations and Freedom) who is known for his opposition to Islam, called the influx of people an "Islamic invasion" during a debate in the Dutch parliament, speaking about "masses of young men in their twenties with beards singing <i>Allahu Akbar</i> across Europe".<sup id="cite_ref-337" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-337"><span>[</span>335<span>]</span></a></sup> He also dismissed the idea that people arriving in Western Europe via <a href="/wiki/Western_Balkans" title="Western Balkans" class="mw-redirect">Western Balkans</a> are genuine refugees, stating: "Turkey, Greece, Macedonia, Serbia are safe countries. If you flee them then you are doing it for benefits and a house."<sup id="cite_ref-338" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-338"><span>[</span>336<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
